      赐下的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      尚方宝剑
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有恃无恐，一时间杀气弥漫，人心惶惶。一些在土地改革中上台斗过地主
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      或分过地主房屋、田地、财产的人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      或与五类分子有过火磨擦的人，都如临大敌
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      大都由地下搬到楼上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      并在楼门口准备了砍刀、棍棒、石块、尿桶和石灰、砂罐之类
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      作为防卫武器。有的在要道上设关立卡
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      派专人日夜防守
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      盘查过往行人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      见生人就抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      发现怀疑对象或打或杀；有的村庄集中起居，并派人去周边邻近各地探查消息
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以便早作准备。更多的大队为防止
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      阶级敌人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，将“地、富、反、坏、右”等“五类分子”及其子弟
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      平时爱提意见不服领导的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      长期在外搞副业的人员
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以及有各种各样“问题”的人员
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      全部集中起来
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      办学习班
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，实行刑讯逼供，脚镣手铐，捆绑吊打，致伤、致残、致死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抓“黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      之风愈演愈烈。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “八·四血案”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      后，中和公社弄子口大队最早行动。该队党支书陈善劝、“文革”主任蒋金祥、治安主任陈春锦（注：陈春锦原是县公安局干部，曾因违法乱纪、逼死人命受到处分，于
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1962
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年退职回家）三人在一个军属家里喝酒，听一个女人说
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      地主子弟
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      陈法林、陈儒成（
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1949
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年参加人民解放军，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      19
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      52
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年转业到甘肃省国营银光化学材料厂
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      即
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      805
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      厂，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      62
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年因病带
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      30%
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的工资回乡）两人在
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      打禾桶边起拱子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      （邵阳土话，即阴谋闹事之意），立即抓捕讯问，二人拒不承认欲
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      阴谋起事
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。于是陈善劝等人率民兵将陈法林、陈儒成推到屋后山上，由治安主任持刀剖腹，未死，又用鸟铳将二人打死。此后又将从山西抓回的地主子弟陈儒林用乱棍打死。在不到一个月的时间内，该队先后共打、杀
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，迫使
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      2
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人自杀，成了全县在抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运动中杀人最早、死人最多的大队之一。
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn7" name="_ednref7" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [7]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      据塘田市区后来调查汇报：塘田市公社三角大队
     </span>
     <st1:chsdate day="12" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False" month="8" year="1968">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       1968
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       年
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       8
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       12
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       日
      </span>
     </st1:chsdate>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      召
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      开大队党支部会，支书唐远亚说，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      当前阶级斗争极其复杂紧张，许多地方出现了‘黑杀队’。难道我们这里没有？石门片的唐宋保常跑东安，这股风就是从东安传来的，难道他没有问题？
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      会议提出，把三角片的唐建勋、唐庭方抓起来审向。为统一思想，第二天又召开了各生产队长、共产党员、贫协和“造反派”负责人会议，统一分
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      工，抓人审向，方法就是捆绑吊打。唐建勋由于绳索吊断，重重地摔落在地上，头皮跌破，鲜血直流，不省人事。有人说：捉虎容易放虎难，不如弄死算了。于是指派了几个地主分子，将唐建勋抬到兔子山桐子坪大漏岩里活埋了。石门片的唐宋保被抓后遭酷刑吊打，供出
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队头目
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      唐慧方，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      秘书
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      唐岛生，还有出身不好的唐运阳、唐运生、唐方雄等；进一步逼供，又得到
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要杀某某党员、某某干部、某某贫协等供词。
     </span>
     <st1:chsdate day="20" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False" month="8" year="2009">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       8
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       20
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       日
      </span>
     </st1:chsdate>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，该片即召开党员、干部、贫协和
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      造反派”负责人会议，研究如何处理
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      成员，会议决定将这些人处死。
     </span>
     <st1:chsdate day="21" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False" month="8" year="2009">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       8
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       21
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       日
      </span>
     </st1:chsdate>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，由支委唐运雨主持会议，宣布唐岛生、唐运阳、唐运生死刑，立即执行。会后由民兵将三人押送到芙夷江畔，推入河中淹死。唐岛生是台胞林月竹生于台湾岛上的儿子，故名“岛生”，本想送回故乡成家立业，服务乡梓，谁知遭此横祸，死时年仅
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      22
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      岁。
     </span>
     <st1:chsdate day="22" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False" month="8" year="2009">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       8
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       22
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       日
      </span>
     </st1:chsdate>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，唐慧方、唐宋保也被推入河中淹死了。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      越刮越凶，不少生产队干部组织农民到邻近市县抓本地在外工作的“五类分子”子弟。不少地方杀人后处理尸体的方式是往河里一丢了事。邵阳县处于资江上游，因此资江河下游河段的死尸日夜漂流不息，引起下游城市邵阳市民众极大震恐。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 24pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      邵阳县“支左办”的军代表柴德林对杀人之风的蔓延负有不可推卸之责任。据邵阳县公安局罗金陵等人回忆：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      6
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      日
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，柴
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: red;">
      德林
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      去电
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将部分徒步去韶山参观的政法干部紧急召回开座谈会
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。会上，柴
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      介绍了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抓黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的情况后强调说：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      对死人问题
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      你们不要指责
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不要追究责任
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      更不要向群众泼冷水。”他说：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      这是群众运动
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      群众专政。群众专政是新生事物
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      是天然合理的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他还说：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫下中农是最高人民法院
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      打死几个阶级敌人算不了什么
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      打死不是白打死了。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他还要求每个政法干部去买一本毛泽东的《湖南农民运动考察报告》单行本
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      好好学习
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ‘
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      好得很’和‘糟得很’的问题
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      争当
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ‘
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      好得很’派
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      而不要去当
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ‘
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      糟得很
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ’
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      派
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。他还提醒干部：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      如果你们去指责制止
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      农民就会把你们也当成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ‘
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队’杀了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      或丢到河里去
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      我也救不了你们。”他把全体政法干部分成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个小组下到各区社
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      观阵
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。县公检法领导说：目前全县抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抓出了几十个
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命组织
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      线索
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      你们下去也要查一查
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      掌握一点情况
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不要让人将其杀掉
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以免断线
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不利于一网打尽。可是政法干部下去后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      只听一片杀人声
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      任何劝止、忠告
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      那怕说
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      政策规定杀人权在省里
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      都不起任何作用
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      因为每个区社都由武装部长掌权
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      而每个区社武装部长又都握有县“支左办”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      柴
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      政委的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      尚方宝剑
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。在这种情况下
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      政法干部实在无能为力
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      只能眼睁睁地干着急。区社干部靠边站
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      参加
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      三支二军”的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      47
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      军驻军部队多次派官兵下乡，做艰苦细致的思想工作
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      强调不准任意抓人、打人、杀人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      搞
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      形左实右
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      严防阶级敌人搅乱阶级阵线，都无济于事
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反而越杀越凶。到
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月中旬
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      乱砍滥杀之风更为严重
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      许多地方见生人就抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有怀疑就杀。在这种混乱局面中
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不少人乘机为非作歹，有公报私仇的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有挟嫌报复的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有趁火打劫的，形势混乱到了极点。
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn8" name="_ednref8" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [8]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      4.
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      野蛮残忍至极的杀人手段
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要了解
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年邵阳县抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”这一滥
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杀运动的残酷性，还必须了解所谓“贫下中农最高人民法院”杀人手段的残忍。当时常见的杀人手法有活埋、“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      铳决”
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn9" name="_ednref9" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [9]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、石砸
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      吊麻蛏（
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      guai
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，去声，邵阳方言，将青蛙称作麻蛏）
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn10" name="_ednref10" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [10]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      耙（锄）头挖
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、捆绑
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      沉河
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      乱棍打死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      绳索勒死等方法，通常死后对尸体不加掩埋，甚至不许其亲属收尸。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不过，在所有稀奇古怪的杀人手法中，上述几种还算比较“文明”的。以下各种让人在死前受尽各种折磨的杀人方法，则显示了杀人者的残酷阴暗心理
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       擀面条
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黄亭市公社金锋大队一个学生
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      期间
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      去邵阳市办事
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被诬以为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      搬救兵
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，民兵们
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      强令其俯睡在木凳上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      背脊上横放一根铁棍
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      铁棍两端各坐一人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在其身体上压过来压过去
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，如同
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      擀面条一样
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      几百斤重的压力
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      之下，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      只压得这位学生屎尿直流，骨头断裂而亡。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       铁丝穿脚筋
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      长阳铺公社长阳铺大队下街生产队社员刘利民被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在他家里挖地三尺
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      寻找枪枝弹药和反革命罪证
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，并
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      对刘的家人画地为牢
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      白天不准出门
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      晚上不准点灯。最后民兵用烧红的铁丝穿过刘利民的一双脚筋
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      吊到门前阶檐梁上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      再活活打死。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       脑袋开花
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      县五中学生邓爱毛被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      后，被人绑在学较的篮球架上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      再用带铁钉的木棒外包橡皮敲脑袋
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一敲几个洞
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打一片红
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，杀人者将此方法命
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      名为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      脑袋开花
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       铁锤锤手臂
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      小溪市公社山伏冲大队贫农社员罗顶名被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      批斗时民兵将他的手腕强按在青砖上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      再用油榨坊里捶枯饼用的两个大铁锤轮流捶打
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      双手骨头被生生捶得粉碎
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，最后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一锤送命。该公社梅洲大队地主子弟罗尧立
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被打成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被人用老虎钳子将手指夹粉
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      然后将他杀死丢到河里。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       火烧
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黄塘公社合兴大队泥工师傅邓玉枚被打成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      酷刑逼供
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      上吊下烧
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，最后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被活活烧死，场景极为残酷。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       烙铁烙
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      国营河伯岭林场马头岭工区贫协主任罗顶有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，系中
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      共党员
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。“文革”初期
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      曾担任过一个群众组织的头头
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      28
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      日，当地一伙人把他当成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      成员捆绑吊打
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将其右臂打断后，又用柴刀把他的脊梁骨砍断
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，然后再将罗的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      左臂按在石板上用铁锤将骨头锤碎
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，再
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用烧红的烙铁在吕身上烙
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      烙得流油冒烟
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，其状惨不忍睹。随后，这伙人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      把罗吊在树上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，直至
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      快断气时方才放下来，剥光衣服
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      倒拖双脚丢到河沟里
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，再
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用乱石砸死。罗妻在当地无法生活
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，被迫
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将大儿子送人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      自己带着小女儿改嫁他乡。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      九公桥中学教师钟明良，家庭出身地主
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在“文革”中一度比较活跃。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫宣队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      （“ 贫下中农毛泽东思想宣传队”的简称）进
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      驻学校，钟被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      关押了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      13
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      天
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      关押期间
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      受尽酷刑，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      先把他捆绑放在一间小屋里
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      令学生们在楼上向他撒尿
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      名曰
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      坐尿牢
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。之后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      又把他双手向后反剪捆绑倒挂
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      面向一盆大水
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      绳索一松
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      头即浸入水中呛水
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      过一会儿再把绳头一拉
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      使头部脱离水面
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      如此拉拉放放
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      多次反复
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      名曰
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      顺手牵羊喝水
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。此外还用了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      荡秋千
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      铁丝穿手掌
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      等十几种酷刑。“贫宣队”中有人说
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他还有个漂亮的老婆
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不要放过他
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      于是有人又想出了一个毒招
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用烧红的烙铁烙钟的生殖器，钟受尽酷刑而死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      时年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      34
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      岁。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       脖子上挂水桶，肚子上压土砖
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      罗城公社毛坪大队豺狗山生产队贫协组长、共青团员曾桂林
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      24
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      岁
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，“文革”初期
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      担任过一个群众组织的负责人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      日
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在大队关押
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      24
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      天。刑讯逼供中，民兵将曾桂林的双手反绑吊起
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      来，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      再在其脖子上挂一桶水
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      身上压几块土砖
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      活活拷打致死。其双目失明的老父曾国奉不知儿子已被打死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，摸索着
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将仅有的一只老母鸡杀了煮好来送饭
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。民兵
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      们恶狠狠地把鸡夺过来倒在地上喂狗，老人想摸摸儿子的尸体都不获准，气得爬在地上咬土喊天。这伙人还把曾的家产抄劫一空
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      把老人赶出家门
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      土改时分的房子也被人霸占了。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      <b>
       “
      </b>
     </span>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       五马
      </span>
     </b>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
     </b>
     <b>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       分尸
      </span>
     </b>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      檀江公社税务干部蒋意兴，邵阳县水田公社人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      家庭出身地主
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队”揪回家乡批斗之后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，再
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被押到一座竹山里
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      由五个民兵分别将不同方向的五根竹子扳弯吊下来
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      再将蒋的头、双手和双脚分别捆到五根竹子尖上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      然后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      五个人齐声高喊：一、二、三
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将绑了人的五根竹子尖同时放开
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      蒋这个活生生的人当即被五根竹子的弹力撕成碎片。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以上记述的杀人手法，于史料而言绝非可有可无之闲笔。设若中国文明进步，这一页耻辱的历史或使国人产生自省之心。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      与人类历史上任何灾难一样，在受害者当中，女性所受的凌辱较男性更多。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      五丰铺公社板桥大队回乡女知青吕小苏
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      家庭出身地主
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。本人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      长相姣好
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      追求者甚多。但她心高气傲
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      对本乡本土的人全不放在眼里
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      高中毕业后与一个大学生恋爱，择日成亲。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月新婚之夜，被本村一伙垂涎欲滴者诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      从新房中抓出批斗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      毒打不屈
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被这伙人把衣服剥光
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      并在其乳房和私处乱摸乱捏
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      吕不甘受辱
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      破口大骂
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      流氓、畜牲
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不得好死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。垂涎者脑羞成怒
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      恶狠狠地说：我得不到的东西别人也休想得到。然后用铁丝穿其乳头
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      丢到板桥水坝中淹死。黄塘公社有个妇女在邵阳市某小学当炊事员，只因家庭出身地主，被当成“黑杀队”揪回批斗，并要处死，她向打手们求情，说：我学校里床头的稻草中有个存折，存有几百元钱，请你们拿去，饶我一命。凶手们如莸至宝，立即奔赴学校，将她的宿舍进行大搜查，存折到手，立即返回，几个人对其实施轮奸后，说：此人留不得，活口祸害多。便偷偷地将她活埋了。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在这场屠杀当中，人性中最阴暗的丑恶被激活了，一些生产大队的干部与民兵不仅以杀人为乐，还要凭借其淫威制造骨肉相残的人伦惨剧。长乐公社新石村的罗光楚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1949
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年以前
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      教私塾为业，抗日战争时期曾当过两年保长
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      土改时家庭成份划为“小土地出租”。“文革”中他被人诬指为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，虽受尽各种酷刑，直至皮裂骨折筋断，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      奄奄一息，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      仍然不肯招认这一莫须有的罪名。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      该队干部将其做铁匠的儿子叫来，说：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      你父亲是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ‘
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队员’
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      现行反革命分子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      你是可以教育好的子女，能不能与他划清界线？看你把他如何处理？
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      小铁匠被逼得走投无路
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      只好强忍悲痛
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      横下心来，在众目暌暌之下
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      噙着满眶热泪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      把垂死的老父亲往肩上一杠
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      走到小河边
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      狠心往河里一抛
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      让其父亲随波逐流而去。双清公社比田大队刘家生产队张南卿（中农成份）被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队员”后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，受尽酷刑，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      干部们强令张的两个弟弟将张丢到老煤窑里窒息而死。这种逼迫亲人下手杀亲人的方式可谓丧尽天良，既使生者蒙受丧亲之痛，还要让他们承担巨大的道德心理压力。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      小溪市公社活水坑大队生产队长蒋柳桥
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      男
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫农
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。“文革”初期
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      因参加名叫
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      资江烽火
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的群众组织，于
     </span>
     <st1:chsdate day="12" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False" month="9" year="1968">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       1968
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       年
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       9
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       12
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       日
      </span>
     </st1:chsdate>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，在公社机关
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被加上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      脚镣手铐关了一个多月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中又被关押批斗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用铁钉鞋掌嘴
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用扁担砍腰
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      只打得他遍体鳞伤
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      痛不欲生
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被迫悬梁自缢
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      死后被定为“畏罪自杀”，说他不如一条狗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，并
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      强迫其家属扎个草人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将蒋生前的衣裤套到草人身上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      挂上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      畏罪自杀
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不如一条狗”的牌子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      批斗三天三夜。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      绝大多数死者在被处死之前，都遭受过非人的侮辱。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      小溪市公社活水坑大队贫农社员王有柱，因参加
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      资江烽火
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      群众组织被诬为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，被捕入监，反铐
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      背包狱
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      天
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      夜，因其屎拉在监狱角落里，被看守按住头，踩住脚，逼着把粪吃掉。还有人被酷刑折磨得自杀以明无罪。下花桥区出现一条“打倒毛主席”的标语，被诬
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      学区主任邹仕楚所为，因他出身地主而被怀疑，饱受酷刑，邹受刑不过，被迫拿菜刀当众剖腹
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，让人看自己“心是红的还是黑的”，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      肠胃流了满地，气绝身亡。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的过程中，刑讯手段之残忍，杀人手段之惨无人道，真是不胜枚举，也卒不忍闻。对出面制止或提出不同意见者，杀人者均说是“阶级立场不稳”，与
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      同罪，因此丢命者大有人在。这样一来，谁也不敢过问，任凭暴行泛滥。人们私下形容当时的杀人狂潮：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杀猪要扯税票，杀牛要经批准，只有杀人和杀鸡一样，想杀就杀。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      干部是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      背起包袱下乡，勾起脑壳（低头）走路，吊起脑壳呷饭（意谓命悬一线），日夜提心吊胆
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。这
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      确是当时情况的真实写照。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5.
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      塘田会议，智勇陶柏荣制止杀人风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “黑杀风”延至
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月下旬
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      资江河里漂浮的死尸接二连三
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      死状甚惨，两岸观者云集
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      居于资江下游的邵阳市自来水厂的抽水机莲蓬头也被死尸堵塞
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      水质腥臭。市民逾半月不敢饮用自来水，民众哗然
     </span>
