     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。当时邵阳市既是行署、地委驻跸之地，也是市委、市政府所在地。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      地区民政部门组织了一些小船沿河捞埋尸体
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      每具尸体工费
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      加草席一床裹埋。市公安局也以同样方式派人沿河捞尸
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运到郊外掩埋。邵阳市民怨鼎沸：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      真是黑了天了！（暗无天日之意）”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      这时，一个邵阳地区人民不应忘记的人出现了。
     </span>
     <st1:chsdate day="24" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False" month="8" year="2009">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       8
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       24
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       日
      </span>
     </st1:chsdate>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      解放军
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      47
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      军国防线路施工大队副政委陶柏荣率
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      139
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      师施工连经衡阳、邵东、到达邵阳县境内
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      驻扎在塘田市区国防线路增音站。塘田市杀人风甚炽，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      风声渐传至陶柏荣耳朵里。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      某一天，陶柏荣听说又有人被当成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      打死了，接着看到一队农民气势汹汹地手执各种武器，将被捆绑成一串的多个人往河里推。经询问
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      方知是当地“贫下中农最高人民法院”在处死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队员”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      面对如此血腥的混乱局面
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      地方当局居然装聋作哑，无人过问。陶柏荣出于人的良知，毅然冲破军队不介入地方“文革”的禁条，挺身而出
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      迅速赶到到塘田市区委机关
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      找到区武装部长肖长青和靠边站的区委书记宁
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      斌
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      三人交流情况后商定
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      立即采取紧急措施
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      由部队出面
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      47
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      军师政委的名义
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      召集
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      区、社机关全体干部和各大队主要领导三级干部紧急大会。
     </span>
     <st1:chsdate day="25" islunardate="False" isrocdate="False" month="8" year="2009">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       8
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       25
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       日
      </span>
     </st1:chsdate>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      上午
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      与会人员全部到齐
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      区礼堂座无虚席
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      由陶柏荣政委做报告。陶政委重点强调社会主义法制观念
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      狠批乱抓、乱打、乱杀人的无政府状态
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。他
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      明确指出，乱杀人是极其错误的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      是违法犯罪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      必需立即制止；真正有罪之人也应该交由人民政府依法处理；今后谁再乱杀人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不管他出身如何
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      都要追究法律责任
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以命偿命
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。陶柏荣要求所有与会人员散会后甄别所抓人员，有问题的上交
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      其余的全部释放。陶柏荣作报告时正气凛然
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，态度
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      果敢坚定
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      话语掷地有声
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      震慑力极大。当时全国“军管”，军队威信极高，他那句
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以命还命
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，使那些杀人者意识到后果严重
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。陶柏荣考虑到全县类似的问题可能极其严重
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      自己又军务在身
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      便以师政委的名义与县支左办
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      柴德林
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      政委通了电话
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      通报了塘田紧急会议的情况
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      并要求县领导迅速采取果断措施
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      坚决刹住乱杀人之风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      绝不能任其继续蔓延
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      危害人民。
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn11" name="_ednref11" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [11]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “塘田会议”使炽热的杀人之风得到遏止，并起了很好的示范作用。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      日
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，邵阳
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      县驻军“支左”领导小组及全体官兵迅速召开紧急会议
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      决定以“塘田会议”为榜样
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      进一步研究制止乱杀人问题
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，会上做了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      4
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      条
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      决定：一，严格依法办事
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      维护无产阶级专政的权威和秩序；二，严禁随意抓人杀人；三，区、社不准介绍（本地干部、民兵等）到外地抓人；四，一切在押人员立即无条件释放
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      真正有罪的送县军管小组处理。但因紧接着又大刮所谓的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      红色政治台风”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清理阶级队伍”，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杀人风”与“刮台风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      同时并进
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      直至
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月，肆虐近
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个月之久的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀风”才算基本平息下去。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      制止杀人的陶柏荣是个有胆有识、谋大事不拘小节的人物。数年后，陶柏荣转业到邵阳市，有死里逃生者登门求见，感谢他的救命之恩
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他才将自己当时所冒的风险说了出来：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      那次我也犯了个冒充师政委的错误
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      因为县里也是团级
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      都是同级
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他会听我的吗？幸好当时不戴军衔
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      使我冒充成功
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      回部队后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      我还向师领导作了检讨
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      得到了师首长的谅解和支持
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      才侥幸过了这一关。”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年，地、县联合调查团
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      经过
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一个多月的调查摸底，结果如下：全县在抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运动中，共抓了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      11,177
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，关押
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7,781
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，私设监狱
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      702
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      处，自制镣铐
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1,587
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      付，被打死、杀死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      322
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人、逼迫自杀
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      669
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，共计死亡
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      991
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人；另有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      113
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人致残。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
      三、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
      年滥
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
      杀风再度兴起
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      塘田会议后，大部分地区的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      开始平息。但由于极左路线盘根错节，根深蒂固，有人怕
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      留下活口遭报复
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，务求斩草除根，不留后患。据塘田市区了解，该区在会后又追杀了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      30
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      多人，其他各地也有追杀现象。有的地方则等待时机，准备新账老账一起算。在
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1969
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      斗、批、改
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      （
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      又叫“三分之一”，因为全县的斗、批、改运动计划分三批搞完）运动和
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运动中，又相继发生了捆绑吊打和刑讯逼供等死人事件。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimHei;">
      1.
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      邵阳县革委会主任汪某的“七杀令”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年春
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，全国
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      根据上级的统一部署
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      广泛开展
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      打击现行反革命破坏活动
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反对贪污盗窃、反对投机倒把、反对铺张浪费
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运动，具体到邵阳县，就成了抓“黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的继续。这一年的农历正月初八日
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      邵阳县召开
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3,000
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人的干部大会
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      县革委主任、人武部部长
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      汪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      某在会上声色俱厉
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'MS Mincho';">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杀气腾腾地说：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      这次
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ‘
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ’，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      就是要用无产阶级专政的铁拳头
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将旧社会遗留下来的那些污泥浊水、资产阶级毒瘤
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      也就是那些贪污、盗窃、投机倒把和形形色色的反革命分子、坏分子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以及有各种各样严重问题的人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      全部、干净、彻底地清查出来
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      该抓则抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      该关则关
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      该判则判
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      该杀则杀
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以免他们一有风吹草动就跳出来兴风作浪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      危害社会主义革命和建没。对于这些危害社会的残渣余孽和害群之马
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      绝不能心慈手软
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要下狠心将他们一网打尽
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      斩尽杀绝。”紧接着，注主任一连喊了“杀杀杀杀杀杀杀”等七个“杀”字，说
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要杀出全县城乡一片红
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要杀出一个红彤彤的新世界。”邵阳县全境立即陷入一片惊惶恐怖之中。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      据原和平公社党委书记陆古成回忆
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      会议当晚，该社即有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被吓得自杀身亡。他的回忆足以佐证当时的恐怖气氛：此时县里正筹建氮肥厂，向和平公社布置红砖生产任务，陆古成不该在电话里询问，红砖的价格是按市场价还是按调拨价？结果被县革委会主任在全县电话会上大骂特骂，说他
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      算资本主义帐
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      地地道道的走资派
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，要
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      查他出身九代
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，并
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      撤职查办
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。后来，县委果然派出专案组对陆的家庭出身、社会关系和工作经历明查暗访，彻底调查，结果什么问题也没有查出来。但陆古成为避祸，就此辞职，远走高
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      飞。
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn12" name="_ednref12" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [12]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      2.
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      “学习班”成了阎王殿
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运动分为农村、县城两大块。县直属机关集中财贸、工交、卫生、农、林、水系统干部
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      举办所谓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      三清三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      学习班
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      即清政治、清经济、清思想，反贪污盗窃、反投机倒把、反铺张浪费。学习班地址选在靠近县人武部
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      紧邻芙夷河畔的原县一中校舍。抽调一百多名干部组成专案班子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      再选拔
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      177
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      名贫下中农代表组成“毛泽东思想宣传队”同时参加
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      造反”起家、红得发紫的县革委常委黄明宣负责全盘操作。办学习班前培训骨干时，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      柴
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      政委强调：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      怀疑就是对象
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      交代就是证据
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”，“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      箩索就是逮捕证
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      吊断箩索数现钱。”他还告诫大家：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      林副统帅指示
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      文化大革命有大战役小战役
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      文战役武战役
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      配合进行
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      现在是
     </span>
     <st1:chmetcnv hasspace="False" negative="False" numbertype="1" sourcevalue="200" tcsc="0" unitname="米">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       200
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       米
      </span>
     </st1:chmetcnv>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      拼刺刀的时候了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不要心慈手软
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要把火药味搞得浓浓的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      给他们以致命的打击。”他的行动口号是：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      领导者威风凛凛，指挥者杀气腾腾
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      执行者步步扣紧
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      搞得他们昏昏沉沉。”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      学习班一共开办了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      期
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      先后有两千多人参加
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      由黄明宣一手操作
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。黄
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      仍然沿用抓“黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      刮台风”那一套极左的高压手段
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      动用了集中国酷刑之大成的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      40
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      多种刑罚（
      <span style="color: #c00000;">
       详见附录
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
      1
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ）
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      半数以上人受过多种酷刑
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被逼死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      41
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被毒打致残。群众如此描述这学习班：“四门紧闭站双岗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中间流动背起枪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      大房子设刑场
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      小房子搞审判
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      大礼堂设法场
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      进了一中无有好下场。”在严刑逼供下
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，学习班的人当中有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      82%
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的人被打成贪污、盗窃分子、反革命、或其他坏分子。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      九公桥粮站保管员王克俊
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      60
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      岁
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。在学习班期间，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他经受了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      21
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      种刑罚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      次昏死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      坐黑牢长达一年多
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被毒打致残。后查证落实
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      只有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      34
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元钱账目不清。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黄亭市粮站会计罗庆云
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      家庭成份中农
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      红旗公社红旗大队人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      原怀疑他是只
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      大老虎
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      车轮战术
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      轮番轰炸
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      两天两夜
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      间用尽
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      各种刑罚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。罗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      实在无法熬下去，趁上厕所时用剃须刀片割颈自杀
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      死后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，学习班
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      立即召开大会
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      说罗以自杀向党“示威
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      对抗运动
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      是自绝于人民的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      现行反革命分子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”。还
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      举办了罗的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      罪行展览会”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      从国库取钱取粮
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      派专车从他家里把稍值钱一点的东西
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      包括他妹妹用作嫁妆的被褥
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      全部拉到县城塘渡口做
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      罪证展览
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。更让人奇怪的是，罗死后一年多，即
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1971
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      4
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      日
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      县人保组、军管会还发出“联合通知”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      罗庆云遵纪守法
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      老实改造
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      争取成为新人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。杀人者的草菅人命与漫不经心
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      由此可见一斑。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      李根银
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      下花桥区医院革委会副主任
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      复员军人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      共产党员。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月作为积极分子和接班人来参加学习班。只因在一次夜晚巡逻放哨时说了一句，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      听说中央来政策了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      松了”，就被扣上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      动摇军心”的帽子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      成了“运动的绊脚石”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      批斗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      次后交附近的沙坪大队农民监督改造。李实在想不通
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      割颈自刎。死后被定为“自绝于党、自绝于人民”的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      现行反革命分子”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不准家属收尸
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不准埋棺材
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不准亲友吊唁。当地群众将李的遭遇编成顺口溜：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      头天是红人，二天是罪人，三天是死人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      国营五丰铺林场工人莫益成，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年秋
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      刮台风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      时被打成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      炮打三红
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的“坏头头”，已经被整过一次。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中又被说成是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贪污盗窃
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      分子，新帐老帐一起算。时值严冬，在一个大雪纷飞的晚上，学习班强迫他脱光衣裤，在雪地里接受批斗。这天其妻分娩，无人照管，婴儿被活活冻死。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      学习班的“经济帐”算得更加离奇古怪，旷古未闻：厨师尝菜的咸淡
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      炊事员吃锅巴
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      酿酒工尝酒，药剂员检药、煎药
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      养路工坐车
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      值班员睡公铺
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      屠业员扣秤
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以及出身不好的教师家属按当时的政策享用
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      四属户
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      照顾粮、公费医疗与粮食补差等等
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      都要按工龄长短累进计算
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      高价退赔。一个区机关的炊事员因吃锅巴、尝菜
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，共计
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      退赔
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1,630
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一个屠业员
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'MS Mincho';">
      因
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      卖肉扣秤加罚款共
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9,999
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      因为考虑到上万元就是死罪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，人被
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杀之后就无法收退赔款了。甚至连教师星期天休假
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      也要罚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1.3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元钱一天
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      理由是农民没有星期天（注：当时视工厂所有制不同，学徒工一个月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      18
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      －
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      20
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元，工人一个月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      32
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      －
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      36
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元）
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      县中医院一位姓肖的煎药工
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      62
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      岁
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在学习班上有人质问他说：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      你天天帮病人煎药
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      药中有红枣、桂圆、党参、当归等补药
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      你就没有呷过一点？”肖答：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中药配方有一定的份量
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      哪个敢乱动。”主持人大喊：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不老实
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      吊起来。”肖老头怕吊打
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，心想
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      好汉不吃眼前亏
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      就承认尝过一些甘草、党参。主持人追问：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      究竟呷了多少？”答：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      两三片吧！”片、钱在邵阳话中发音相近。主持人又问：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一天三钱是不是？”老肖心想
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      只要不吊打
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      三钱就三钱，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      于是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      回答说
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。肖老头从事煎药工作共
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年，最后由主持者算帐：一年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      365
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      天
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一天
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      钱
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年就是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      多斤
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年共
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      百多斤
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      甘草、党参各半，按市场高价计算共
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      140
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      多元。结果硬逼肖如数退赔。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      更奇怪的还有：受害者被抓，要出抓人费
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被看管，要出看守费
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被调查，要出脚步费
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被审讯，要出烤火费
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被吊打，要出手续费；连头戴高帽，身穿白褂
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      颈挂黑牌
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      都要按制作成本和加工费，高价算钱。这笔钱没人能够逃交，有的交钱赎人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有的从工资中扣除，还有的在平反复职的补助费中扣除，并说这是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      照章办事”。有个人被关押
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      35
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      天
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      各项费用
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      105.6
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要家属交钱赎人。还有个人被打死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要家属交
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      300
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元领尸
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，死者家贫
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      交不出
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，妻子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被活活气死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，最后还是他
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人帮忙将房屋发卖
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      交了钱才把尸体领回去。有个现役军人回家探亲，看到如此情形，说了句
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      如此搞法不符合党的政策”，立即被戴上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      破坏运动
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的帽子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      坐牢数月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被毒打致残，还被罚跪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      罚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      喝尿。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      教师虽然未参加学习班
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      但也有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      470
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被抓斗审批
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      241
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人惨遭毒打
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被迫自杀。学校并没有什么经济问题
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，黄明宣等人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      便挖空心思
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      亮出
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      高招”：凡剥削阶级家庭出身的教师
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，没有资格
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      享受公费医疗和粮食补差，要按高价退赔
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；其
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      家属在农村按
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      四属户
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      （即干部家属、职工家属、教师家属和军属）吃照顾粮的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      要按自由市场的价格退赔差价
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      星期天未回农村参加农业生产的教师要退赔一天的工资。长乐公社的周凤翔因此退赔
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      314
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      王玉清退赔
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      787
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      赵碧霞退了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      402
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      双江公社的郭雄退赔医疗费
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      290
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      退粮食补差款
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      90
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元。当时小学教师的月工资高的为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      48
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      低的仅
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      32
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      几年不吃不喝也难交完这些退赔账。
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn13" name="_ednref13" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [13]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
      3.
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      农村深挖“反革命集团”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      农村的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以深挖
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命集团
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      为主。据县公安局统计
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      和
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运动中，全县共挖出“反革命组识”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      98
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      起
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      成员
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      744
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      蔡桥公社有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      13
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个大队，其中
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个大队挖出了“反革命组织”：黄亭市公社茶铺大队打出了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个“反革命集团”。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; line-height: 17px; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px; font-family: SimSun;">
      在这些案件中，河伯公社的“五洞反革命集团案”可算是惊天冤案。详情如下：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      此案缘起
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月大抓“黑杀队”之时。当时五洞大队分为两派，互相攻击。有人说地主子弟陈良柱在邻近的东安县打工，抄回了刘伯温的《烧饼歌》和《五公经》，并且秘密传播，这在当时属大逆不道的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命言行
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。大队干部即据此罗织了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
