      以地主子弟陈良柱为首，地主分子陈夷如为后台的反革命集团
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      案，陈良柱被惨杀。两个小小的生产队，折腾得昏天黑地，神哭鬼嚎，县里马上派人帮助破案。在办案过程中，该专案组负责人、县公、检、法军管小组侦破组长陈某某，利用手中的权力，以做思想工作、与所谓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命分子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      划清界线、积极检举揭发为由，对该队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命分子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      陈时元年轻貌美的妻子廖某某威胁利诱，逼迫成奸，而对其夫陈时元则严刑吊打，酷刑问罪，百般折磨致死，廖女被陈霸占长达
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个多月。在此期间，陈某廴发现有谁议论其男女之事，就给谁扣上“反革命分子”的帽子，捆绑吊打，酷刑逼供，投入监牢。结果风言风语越来越多，“反革命集团”也越滚越大，最后在五洞大队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      100
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      户人当中竟有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      96
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      户半成了“反革命”，占
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      96.5%
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      其中这“半户”指陈时元被当作“反革命分子”长期关押致死，其妻廖某某既被陈长期霸占，便被排除在“反革命”之外。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      这个
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命集团
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中计有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      30
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被严刑拷打逼供，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      18
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被逮捕入狱，最长的坐牢
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      28
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个月，最短的也坐了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个月；
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被判刑，刑期短的判了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      4
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年，长的判了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      20
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年，其中
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      6
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人致死，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人致残。这就是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      五洞反革命集团案
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杀夫奸妻案
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。由于“反革命分子”特多，本队的社员要分散交外队管制、监督，同时还要请外队人到本队来当队长。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      这一耸人听闻的冤案从
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      开始，于
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1969
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年“斗、批、改”当中定案，当地干部、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      群众受苦之深，冤屈之重，罄竹难书。此案虽经受害人（即被该干部霸占的陈时元之妻廖某某）多次反映上诉，又经正县级离休干部张必烈等
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人查证核实，但因派性干扰等种种原因，直至
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      80
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年代末全案才获平反，而后，当事人陈某某已死，只好不了了之。
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn14" name="_ednref14" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [14]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 23.05pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黄塘公社有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个知识青年参加修水轮泵站非常卖力，被群众誉为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      八大金刚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。因
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人特别团结，有人便怀疑他们可能有不轨行为，公社
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反办”旋将其定为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命组织
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，名称就是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      八大金刚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。抄家时抄出一张
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      合影照片，以此为
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命集团
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的“证据”，又将一首自勉诗说成是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反动纲领
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，一张寿筵入席名单说成是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命组织
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      成员名单。在
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      如山铁证
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      面前，这
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      8
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个人被打得遍体鳞伤，死去活来。结果查了半年，什么“反革命活动”都未查出来。谷州公社的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个下乡知青因晚上喜欢聚在一起散步谈心，也被怀疑是搞
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命活动
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，画地为牢，惨遭横祸。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      那时整人的花样百出，什么残酷，什么刺激“新鲜”，就用什么。在
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      运动中，双清公社双龙大队院子生产队贫农张自卫被指控为“与反革命有牵连”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，遭到
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      种种酷刑均不肯“认罪”。有人便想出一个毒招：让张屁股半蹲
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      双腿微屈
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      如同打拳的坐桩一般
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      脚板下各放青砖一块
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      双膝上再各放土砖一砣
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      屁股下面的土地上插梭标一柄
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      标尖向上，对准屁股
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      脖子吊在一根垂直的箩索上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      再用两根稻草把两个大姆指吊起来
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      名曰“练功桩”，两分钟不到人就昏厥。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抓经济问题，整人整得更惨。例如，和平公社新河大队张十延是个祖传牙医
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      技术好，医德佳
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      很受人欢迎
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。他
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      与生产队签订合同外出镶牙
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      按规定缴款。运动中说他在外
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      搞投机倒把
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”，走
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      资本主义道路，赚钱盖新房
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将其关押批斗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，其所有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      财产包括新砌的房屋在内一律没收充公。小溪市公社文昌大队赤脚医师简雪波，在运动中被指控为“有经济问题”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      新生的资本主义
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      典型，被关在大队部办“学习班”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      后来惨死在被关押的小屋里。河伯岭林场马头岭工区妇女主任邓细妹怀有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      个月身孕
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中遭诬陷
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      强迫她脱光衣裤坐在装满水的大澡盆里
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      名曰
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      坐水牢
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”，最后被
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      活活折磨而死。陈勋尧是河伯公社上阳大队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      19
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      生产队人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫农，曾贩卖过几疋土布
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中被当作
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      投机倒把分子
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      批斗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      背脊骨被打断
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      睾丸被捅烂
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      疼痛难忍
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      上吊自尽。死后当地干部不准家属哭
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不准送葬
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      还要在棺材上贴上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反革命分子陈勋尧死鬼灭魂
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的字条
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      勒令他儿子陈上喜照着念
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      念完后还要高喊
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      打倒反革命分子陈勋尧
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的口号。谢习之乃九公桥公社湘河大队人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫农
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      篾匠，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1962
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年起外出搞副业
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      每年按规定缴款投资
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      未欠集体分文。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1970
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年搞
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      县革委会”工作组进驻该队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      将他定为“资本主义典型”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      算了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      笔
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      剥削
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      帐：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年中先后带徒弟
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      6
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      每人每年算雇工剥削
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      180
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      共
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3,240
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      按
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      60%
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      退赔，计
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1,944
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元；在外给人打晒簟
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      936
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      床
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      每床暴利
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      0.5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      计
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      468
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元；在新宁县花
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      500
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元买了一座旧屋架子回家修屋
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      剩余部份木料
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      做了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      4
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      副棺材
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      出卖
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      2
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      副
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      得
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      230
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      重罚
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      500
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      项合计
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      2,916
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，责成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      立即退赔。谢思量全部家当也没有这个数
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被逼悬梁自尽。刘再兴是新建公社新民大队团支部副书记
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫农，回乡知青，因爱提意见被人怀恨在心。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      时被诬为反革命
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      关入烤烟房
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      打得遍身鳞伤
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他咬破手指写血书
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      说自己不是“反革命”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。被
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      释放后的一天
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      刘正在理发
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被人叫去大队部
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一个多小时以后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被吊死在梁上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不但无人追查其死因，反而将其宣布为“反革命”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      为其画相供大队和生产队批斗。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以上只是少数几例。全县农村的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      历时一年，共有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      19,721
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人受到迫害
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      其中贫下中农
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      17,016
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，约占受打击人数的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      90%
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      6,417
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被关押
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      15,340
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被打成“贪污盗窃投机倒把分子”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      定性金额
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      123
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      万多元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抄家
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1.6
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      万户
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抄走各项财产无数
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      307
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被迫害致死
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      91
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人被打成残废
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不少人被整得倾家荡产、流离失所、家破人亡。这是邵阳县继
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抓黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      刮台风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的又一次浩劫。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; letter-spacing: -1pt;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimHei;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
      四、充满荆棘的冤案平反之路
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: SimHei;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 23.25pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      与其它地方相比，邵阳县的政治运动的残酷与多发均属罕见。但这些运动早已使当地政界的人际关系异常复杂，形成一个个利益死结。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年试图平反冤案而做了第一个“吃螃蟹”的勇者杨荫甫还因此蒙受不白之冤。在这种局面下，当全国大多数地区的冤假错案已经平反时，只有邵阳县还徘徊在历史罪错的阴影之中。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      1.
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      年冤案调查，查冤案者反蒙冤
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 23.25pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1973
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年杨荫甫任邵阳县委书记时，曾经给邵阳县带来过一缕短暂的春风。杨荫甫是河北省滦县人，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1949
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      3
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月随军南下，历任邵东县区委书记、县公安局长、县委书记。“文革”初被打倒，下放到农场喂猪。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1972
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月，调邵阳县任县革委副主任，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1973
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月改任县委书记。这种经历使杨荫甫与邵阳县的政治势力无任何利益关系，能够比较客观地看待当地的政情。更重要的是，从
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年抓“黑杀风”以来，一直在邵阳县主政的柴德林此时退居二把手位置。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      <br/>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杨
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      荫甫
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      履任之后，发现邵阳县的极左问题极其严重，在“抓黑杀队”等各项运动中死人上千，仅次于以滥杀闻名于世的湖南道县，遗留下来的政治恩怨更是纠结牵缠，民怨郁积。这些情况使杨荫甫寝食难安，他多方奔走，获地区领导批准，组织联合调查团，第一次大胆地摸了这个极左路线的“老虎屁股”。当时确定的调查措施及后续措施有二：第
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一、对农村组织地、县联合调查团，分期分批调查摸清抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的死人情况，再依法处置；第二、对机关单位
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中被错误地开除的干部适当收回，重新安排工作。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      但一则由于当时全国的政治大气候仍然是极左当道，二则因为邵阳县的极左路线一向较其它地区更甚，多年的政治斗争使利益关系盘根错节，情况格外复杂。杨主持的调查处处受到掣肘。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 23.25pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      4
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月，由
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      100
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      余名干部组成的调查团用一个多月的时间，对全县自
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年以来
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      前后所发生的滥杀事件，包括
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      刮红色政治台风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清理阶级队伍
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      和
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      在内，做了一次全面调查。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      日，中共邵阳地委正、副书记，邵阳军分区司令员、政委等地方军政要员齐集邵阳县委，听取调查团的汇报。一条条人命、一桩桩血案，使得领导们喉哽鼻塞，热泪盈眶，一致表示要坚决落实党的政策，纠正极左遗患，地委将从财政上予以大力支持。中共邵阳地委还以
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      14
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      号绝密文件向中共湖南省委及中共中央汇报。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      同年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月，调查组把
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抓黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      和
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中使用过的刑罚，筛选、汇集成
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      72
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      种，再用一尺见方的硬纸板，用漫画形式绘制成“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      72
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      种刑罚图”，公开展出。结果大受欢迎，大家一致要求由县总工会牵头，组织汇报团，带着“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      72
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      种刑罚图”层层上访，既向各级领导机关详细汇报、展出，又能收到较好的直观效果。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月初，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人汇报团组成，由张介山、尹邦宋负责，从地、市到省，层层组织大中型汇报会，场场爆满，反响极为强烈，纷纷要求将责任人绳之以法。时任湖南省副省长的孙国治表示：问题一定要彻底解决。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      汇报团于
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      14
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      日到达北京后，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      找到党中央、国务院和“中央文革”接待站，该站人员听说是汇报一个县的情况，十分热情，由站领导亲自听取汇报，整整听了一天，边听、边问、边记， 非常认真负责。接待站负责人最后表态：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一个县死了那么多人，那个主要领导是要负责任的，我先给你们省里打个招呼，要他们调查处理上报，再将你们的汇报材料整理成书面文件，上报党中央，请你们先回县里等候消息。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      谁知
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      汇报团
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      回县后左等右等，什么消息也没有等到。这期间发生了一件怪事，“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      72
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      种刑罚图”被人从北京的招待所偷走了，据说至今还收藏在邵阳县公安局的档案柜里，当作一颗
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反党、反社会主义的重磅炮弹
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，准备
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      秋后算账
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年冬，冤案调查工作有了眉目，被错误
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      开除的职工也收回了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      300
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      多人（不到被错误开除总人数的三分之一）。然而，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      全国
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      批极左
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的大气候却转了向，左祸又成熊熊之势。于是，在邵阳一种说法占了主导地位：调查
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      否定无产阶级文化大革命的伟大成果
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      为牛鬼蛇神翻案
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；杨荫甫是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      反党乱军的派头头、派书记
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      。于是，以
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫下中农
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      为名的告状信不断向地委、省委飞去。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1975
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      5
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月，没有地方势力根基的杨荫甫被迫调离邵阳县。这项意在寻公义、正人伦的调查，也为杨此后的仕途埋下了“地雷”，成为他后来屡屡挨整的主要原因。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1976
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年冬，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      四人帮
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      被粉碎。这本来是给极左路线的当头一棒，在
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清查与
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ‘
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      四人帮
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ’
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      有牵连的人和事
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      时，省委向邵阳县这个
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      文革重灾区
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      派出了工作组。但该工作组却依靠邵阳县委坚持极左路线的原班人马，给反极左的原县委书记杨荫甫硬戴上
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      四人帮黑干将
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的大帽子。他们声称：
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年杨荫甫在邵阳县的所作所为，是向‘四人帮’提供进攻中国共产党的黑炮弹，就是篡党夺权，就是为地、富、反、坏、右翻案，做了蒋介石想做而做不到的事。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      从此，杨荫甫成了邵阳地区的头号清查对象，后被撤职，留党察看两年，调省医药工业研究所守大门。邵阳地委同时还宣布：将
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1974
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年杨荫甫主持的有关抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      等的调查报告、领导讲话、工作简报、统计数字及其他一切有关资料，通统作废并彻底销毁处理。结果，凡是参与或支持地、县联合调查团调查过
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的人，都成了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      杨荫甫之流
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      或
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      四人帮的残渣余孽
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，遭批斗、拘捕，甚至被投入监牢。笔者亦是其中之一。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 24pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1978
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年以后，全国各地都在大力“拨乱反正”，“地、富”“摘帽”，“右派”“纠正”，彻底平反冤、假、错案。而中共邵阳县委反而利用
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清查”的机会，以
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      积极参与并支持大乱邵阳县篡党夺权活动
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的罪名，多次下发文件，处理干部
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      14
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，其中撤职
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，党纪或政纪处分
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      4
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，进一步制造出一批冤、假、错案。
     </span>
     <a href="#_edn15" name="_ednref15" style="color: purple;" title="">
     </a>
     <span style="vertical-align: super;">
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       <span style="vertical-align: super;">
        <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
         [15]
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 10pt; margin-left: 0cm; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 23.25pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      不过，杨荫甫主持的调查毕竟为邵阳县
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年抓“黑杀队”以来制造的各种冤假错案，留下了极其宝贵的历史资料，这也是笔者写作此文、见证这段痛史的重要材料。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      2.
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
      不彻底的平反冤假错案
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      十一届三中全会后，邵阳县委挂出了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      落实政策领导小组
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的牌子，除了全国皆推行的“右派”“纠正”，“地、富”“摘帽”外，该地还有一项特殊任务，即对“文革”中抓“黑杀队”、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      刮台风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      和
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      中伤亡人员及财产损失作第二次调查摸底。这次的处理方法是：政治上平反，经济上适当补助，全县共补助
      <span style="color: #c00000;">
       币
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
      22,080
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
      元。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      处理极不彻底，依然上访不断，鸣冤不止。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1985
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      6
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      月
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      罗安荣任邵阳县委书记
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      他按照中共湖南省委（
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1985
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ）
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      12
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      号文件的精神，决定对“文革”中抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      等
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一系列
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      乱杀人事件作第三次调查处理。当时，邵阳县的干部们因各自的利益关系，对处理“文革”中的各种乱杀人事件认识差异很大。有的重弹老调说，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      贫下中农杀死几个阶级敌人没有什么了不起，要搞，会影响大局，不利于安定团结
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；而有些出身较好的受害人亲属则扬言，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      政府不管自己管
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      血债要用血来还
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，大有报仇血恨之势，如果任其发展，后果不堪设想。针对这种种思想情况，县委新班子以省委文件为依托反复强调：杀人是严重违法的犯罪行为，依法处理“文革”中的乱杀人事件，是伸张人伦，伸张正义、伸张法纪，伸张大是大非，是对历史负责，对人民负责，对受害人负责，对子孙后代负责的重大举措；“文革”中的乱杀人，是在特定的历史条件下发生的，不能再用以牙还牙的方法来处理，只能在法律的基础上，在政策允许的范围内，公平合理地解决。随后，邵阳县学习、借鉴了道县的经验，组织了
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      230
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人的“专案班子”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      专门从事落实政策工作，对在
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      抓黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      刮台风
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      、
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      和
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      一打三反
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      等运动中的死人问题
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，作
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      第三次调查摸底。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri; text-indent: 24pt;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      经过这次调查，按照
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      特殊情况
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      宽严适度
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的原则
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      邵阳县重点立案查处乱杀人事件
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      134
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      起
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ；查处
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      主要责任人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      280
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清查后定性处理
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      242
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人（其中追究刑事责任的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      19
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      起，责任人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      30
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，纪律处分
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      217
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      其中开除党籍
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      128
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      留党察看
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      63
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人）；受处分人员中
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      国家干部
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      34
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      开除出党
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      11
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      留党察看
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      9
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人，农村党员受处分的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      208
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      其中大队以上干部
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      152
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      定为杀人罪的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      117
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      犯严重错误的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      19
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人；因主要责任人巳死或责任分散未立案查处的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      92
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      起；对
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      947
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      位受害者彻底平反昭雪
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      恢复名誉
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      用县政府红头文件发平反通知书；对死者遗属按不同情况
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      分别
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      实行常年分月补助，对致伤致残者发定期生活补助费，有房屋和财产损失的
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      原物在的退原物
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      原物不在或受损的折价赔偿，被迫外逃者照样安排田土山水
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      以便其回乡安居乐业；对有特殊困难的遗属
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      批准解决农转非
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      7
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      户
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      招工商户
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      2
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      人。原县委常委、县委副书记、县政协主席黄明轩
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      原区委副书记蒋昭元
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      属于“造反”起家的干部，按“
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      清查三种人
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”的原则处理，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      撤销一切职务，开除党籍。而在
      <span style="color: #c00000;">
       杀人事件中负有主要领导责任的
      </span>
      <span style="color: red;">
       柴德林政委，
      </span>
      <span style="color: #c00000;">
       因邵阳县的干部民众对其怨恨颇深，无法立足，早于
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
      1977
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
      年
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
      12
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
      月调离了邵阳县，迁回其老家黑龙江省呼兰县。对其“文革”草菅人命之罪，有关方面并未给予任何处理。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      直至
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1987
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年底，对邵阳县始于
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1968
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”以来的系列杀人事件的追究处理
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      才算基本告一段落。“文革”在中国的结束时间是
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      1976
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年，而邵阳县平反“文革”期间大规模杀人冤案，却比“文革”结束晚了将近
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      10
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      年。在邵阳县，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      从冤案始直至平反，前后
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      经历了八届县委领导
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ，其间种种政治较量，
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的确耐人寻味。更令人不满的是，当年首倡调查“抓
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      黑杀队
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      的杨荫甫等一大批干部，曾因
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      “
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      篡党夺权
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      ”罪名被
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      撤职或遭党纪、政纪处分，他们至今未获任何甄别，更谈不上对他们落实政策。当时对他们作错误处理的文件，至今仍然保存在这些受冤干部的档案袋里。“文革”过去已
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      30
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      多年了，但在邵阳“文革”余毒至今依然存在。
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
      注释
     </span>
     <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      :
     </span>
    </p>
   </div>
   <div style="color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; letter-spacing: normal; font-size: medium;">
    <br clear="all"/>
    <hr align="left" size="1" width="33%"/>
    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
      <a href="#_ednref1" name="_edn1" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [1]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       《邵阳县志》第
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       554
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       页，社会科学文献出版社（北京），
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       1993
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       年
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       6
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月出版。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
     </p>
    </div>
    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">

      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [2]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">

      </span>

      </span>

      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">

         </span>

      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       年
      </span>

       4
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月邵阳地区、邵阳县联合调查团，《调查材料记实》。本文所引资料凡未注明出处者，均出自《调查材料记实》。
      </span>

    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
      <a href="#_ednref5" name="_edn5" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [5]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       1981
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       年
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       5
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       月．因县属金江水厍占地矛盾长期难以解决，该队已由东安县划归邵阳县管辖，成为金江水厍管理区之一。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">

      <a href="#_ednref6" name="_edn6" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [6]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>

       张介山，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
