    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
      <a href="#_ednref7" name="_edn7" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [7]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       李进华，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       邵阳县
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ‘
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       文革
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ’
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       黑杀风始末
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ，载《为了邵阳的安宁》，中共邵阳市委党史研究室编写，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       2005
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       年出版。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
     </p>
    </div>
    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
      <a href="#_ednref8" name="_edn8" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [8]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       罗金林，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       回忆
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       作者手稿。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
     </p>
    </div>
    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
      <a href="#_ednref9" name="_edn9" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [9]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       铳决
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       一词系邵阳县
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       贫下中农最高人民法院
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       的
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       创造
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       。调查组在邵阳县塘田市区发现一张
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       布告
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ：
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
       ｘｘｘ，男，现年
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       38
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
       岁，家庭成份地主。一贯与贫下中农作对，现参加
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ‘
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
       黑杀队
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ’
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
       ，要杀害贫下中农。抓捕后顽固到底，拒不认罪，经大队贫下中农最高人民法院核准死刑，立即执行铳决。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       1968
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
       年
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       8
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: KaiTi_GB2312;">
       月ｘ日
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       。当问及
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       铳决
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       一词的来历时，有人振振有词地说：政府杀人用
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       枪决
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ，我们农民没有枪，只好用
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       铳决
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       了。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
     </p>
    </div>
    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
      <a href="#_ednref10" name="_edn10" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [10]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       此刑详情如下：将人先紧紧捆成粽子形状
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       再用长绳从桥上吊下去
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       一放一提
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       象吊青蛙一样，以折磨取乐
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       。调查组发现的案例中，有用此法将人折磨够了后，再
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       放到溪水里用撑船的篙竿（上有长长的铁尖）捅死。如邵阳县长乐公社贫农社员王青治即死于此刑。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
     </p>
    </div>
    <div>
     <p class="NoSpacing" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-left: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; font-size: 11pt; font-family: Calibri;">
      <a href="#_ednref11" name="_edn11" style="color: purple;" title="">
      </a>
      <span style="vertical-align: super;">
       <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
        <span style="vertical-align: super;">
         <span style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18px;">
          [11]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       陶柏荣，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       “
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       一件欣慰终身的事
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
       ”
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun;">
       ，
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
       《邵阳晚报》
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
       2005
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
       年
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
       4
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
       月
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
       19
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
       日
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #c00000;">
       10
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: SimSun; color: #c00000;">
       版。
      </span>
      <span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
      </span>
     </p>
    </div>
